			every_country = {

				#set sat system

				# GNSS
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^7 > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^7 }
					}
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_mil_system_idx = 7 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_mil_sat_system_max = global.GNSS_sat_system_max_array^7 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_civ_system_idx = 7 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_civ_sat_system_max = global.GNSS_sat_system_max_array^7 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^6 > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^6 }
					}
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_mil_system_idx = 6 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_mil_sat_system_max = global.GNSS_sat_system_max_array^6 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_civ_system_idx = 6 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_civ_sat_system_max = global.GNSS_sat_system_max_array^6 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^5 > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^5 }
					}
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_mil_system_idx = 5 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_mil_sat_system_max = global.GNSS_sat_system_max_array^5 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_civ_system_idx = 5 }
					set_variable = { var_GNSS_civ_sat_system_max = global.GNSS_sat_system_max_array^5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNSS_satellite_array^4 > global.GNSS_sat_system_min_array^4 }
					}

			every_country = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						nuclear_reactor > 0
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 4 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 4 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_dynamic_modifier = {
									modifier = nuclear_state_modifier
								}
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = nuclear_state_modifier }
					}
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NPROG_completed
						NOT = { original_tag = ISR }
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_start_date < 2001.1.1
								NOT = { original_tag = NKO }
							}
							has_start_date > 2016.1.1
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 3 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 3 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_dynamic_modifier = {
									modifier = nuclear_state_modifier
								}
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = nuclear_state_modifier }
					}
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NPROG_completed
						OR = {
							original_tag = ISR
							AND = {
								has_start_date < 2001.1.1
								original_tag = NKO
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 6 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 6 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_dynamic_modifier = {
									modifier = nuclear_state_modifier
								}
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = nuclear_state_modifier }
					}
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = PER
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 7 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 7 }
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 3 }
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 6 }
						}
						OR = {
							original_tag = USA
							original_tag = SOV
							original_tag = CHI
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 9 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 9 }
					set_variable = { var_nuclear_status_aircraft_cost_factor = 0.25 }
					set_variable = { var_nuclear_status_ship_cost_factor = 0.25 }
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 3 }
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 6 }
						}
						original_tag = ISR
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 10 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 10 }
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 11 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 11 }
					set_variable = { var_nuclear_status_aircraft_cost_factor = 0.3 }
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 3 }
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 6 }
						}
						OR = {
							original_tag = ENG
							original_tag = FRA
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 10 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 10 }
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 12 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 12 }
					set_variable = { var_nuclear_status_aircraft_cost_factor = 0.3 }
					set_variable = { var_nuclear_status_ship_cost_factor = 0.3 }
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 3 }
							is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 6 }
						}
						OR = {
							original_tag = RAJ
							original_tag = PAK
							original_tag = NKO
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 11 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 11 }
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						nuclear_reactor > 0
						# Nuclear-weapon-free zone
						OR = {
							capital_scope = {
								is_on_continent = south_america
							}
							capital_scope = {
								is_on_continent = australia
							}
							capital_scope = {
								is_on_continent = africa
							}
							original_tag = TAJ
							original_tag = TRK
							original_tag = UZB
							original_tag = KYR
							original_tag = KAZ
							original_tag = MON
							original_tag = MEX
							original_tag = BRU
							original_tag = BRM
							original_tag = CBD
							original_tag = IND
							original_tag = LAO
							original_tag = MAY
							original_tag = PHI
							original_tag = SIN
							original_tag = SIA
							original_tag = VIE
						}
					}
					add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 0 }
					add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 0 }
					add_to_variable = { var_nuclear_stability_factor = 0.15 }
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
			}
